  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |// Teselation control
  4 |
  5 |layout (vertices = 4) out;
  6 |
  7 |in VS_OUT {
  8 |	vec2 textureCoord;
  9 |} from_vs[];
 10 |
 11 |out TESC_OUT {
 12 |	vec2 textureCoord;
 13 |} to_tese[];
 14 |
 15 |
 16 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
 17 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
 18 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
 19 |  mat4 projMatrix;
 20 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
 21 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
 22 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 23 |};
 24 |
 25 |void main() {
 26 |	// Propagamos la posicin y la coordenada de textura al shader de evaluacin
 27 |	gl_out[gl_InvocationID].gl_Position = gl_in[gl_InvocationID].gl_Position;
 28 |	to_tese[gl_InvocationID].textureCoord = from_vs[gl_InvocationID].textureCoord;
 29 |
 30 |	vec4 edgeDistance[4];
 31 |	edgedistance[0] = distance(gl_out[gl_InvocationID].gl_Position[0],gl_out[gl_InvocationID].gl_Position[1]);
 32 |
 33 |	/*
 34 |		Calcula aqu los niveles de teselacin
 35 |	*/
 36 |	if (gl_InvocationID == 0) {
 37 |		gl_TessLevelOuter[0] = 64.0;
 38 |		gl_TessLevelOuter[1] = 64.0;
 39 |		gl_TessLevelOuter[2] = 64.0;
 40 |		gl_TessLevelOuter[3] = 64.0;
 41 |
 42 |		gl_TessLevelInner[0] = 64.0;
 43 |		gl_TessLevelInner[1] = 64.0;
 44 |	}
 45 |}

Vertex shader: ../p8/shader.vert
--------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |in vec3 position;
 13 |in vec2 texCoord;
 14 |
 15 |out VS_OUT {
 16 |	vec2 textureCoord;
 17 |} vs_out;
 18 |
 19 |void main()
 20 |{
 21 |	// Tomamos los tres bits menos significativos como la coordenada en X
 22 |	int x = gl_InstanceID & 63;
 23 |	// Y los siguientes tres bits como la coordenada en Y
 24 |	int y = gl_InstanceID >> 6;
 25 |
 26 |	// Posicin de la cmara
 27 |	vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
 28 |	// Clculo distancia entre cmara y vrtice
 29 |	edistance = distance(position, eposition);
 30 |	
 31 |	// Movemos la instancia a su sitio
 32 |	vec3 newpos = position - vec3(float(x) - 32.0, position.y, float(y) - 32.0);
 33 |
 34 |	gl_Position = vec4(newpos, 1.0);
 35 |	vs_out.textureCoord = texCoord + vec2(-x*1/64.0f, y*1/64.0f);
 36 |}
 37 |

Tesselation control shader: ../p8/shader.tesc
---------------------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |// Teselation control
  4 |
  5 |layout (vertices = 4) out;
  6 |
  7 |in VS_OUT {
  8 |	vec2 textureCoord;
  9 |} from_vs[];
 10 |
 11 |out TESC_OUT {
 12 |	vec2 textureCoord;
 13 |} to_tese[];
 14 |
 15 |
 16 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
 17 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
 18 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
 19 |  mat4 projMatrix;
 20 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
 21 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
 22 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 23 |};
 24 |
 25 |void main() {
 26 |	// Propagamos la posicin y la coordenada de textura al shader de evaluacin
 27 |	gl_out[gl_InvocationID].gl_Position = gl_in[gl_InvocationID].gl_Position;
 28 |	to_tese[gl_InvocationID].textureCoord = from_vs[gl_InvocationID].textureCoord;
 29 |	
 30 |	vec3 edgePosition[4];
 31 |	edgePosition[0] = vec3(modelViewMatrix * ((gl_out[gl_InvocationID].gl_Position[0] + gl_out[gl_InvocationID].gl_Position[1]) / 2.0f));
 32 |
 33 |	float edgeDistance[4];
 34 |	edgeDistance[0] = distance(edgePosition[0], vec3(0.0f, 0.0f, 0.0f));
 35 |
 36 |	/*
 37 |		Calcula aqu los niveles de teselacin
 38 |	*/
 39 |	if (gl_InvocationID == 0) {
 40 |		gl_TessLevelOuter[0] = 64.0 / max(edgeDistance[0], 1.0f);
 41 |		gl_TessLevelOuter[1] = 64.0 / max(edgeDistance[0], 1.0f);
 42 |		gl_TessLevelOuter[2] = 64.0 / max(edgeDistance[0], 1.0f);
 43 |		gl_TessLevelOuter[3] = 64.0 / max(edgeDistance[0], 1.0f);
 44 |
 45 |		gl_TessLevelInner[0] = 64.0 / max(edgeDistance[0], 1.0f);
 46 |		gl_TessLevelInner[1] = 64.0 / max(edgeDistance[0], 1.0f);
 47 |	}
 48 |}

Tesselation control shader: ../p8/shader.tesc
---------------------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |// Teselation control
  4 |
  5 |layout (vertices = 4) out;
  6 |
  7 |in VS_OUT {
  8 |	vec2 textureCoord;
  9 |} from_vs[];
 10 |
 11 |out TESC_OUT {
 12 |	vec2 textureCoord;
 13 |} to_tese[];
 14 |
 15 |
 16 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
 17 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
 18 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
 19 |  mat4 projMatrix;
 20 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
 21 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
 22 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 23 |};
 24 |
 25 |void main() {
 26 |	// Propagamos la posicin y la coordenada de textura al shader de evaluacin
 27 |	gl_out[gl_InvocationID].gl_Position = gl_in[gl_InvocationID].gl_Position;
 28 |	to_tese[gl_InvocationID].textureCoord = from_vs[gl_InvocationID].textureCoord;
 29 |	
 30 |	vec3 edgePosition[4];
 31 |	edgePosition[0] = vec3(modelviewMatrix * ((gl_out[gl_InvocationID].gl_Position[0] + gl_out[gl_InvocationID].gl_Position[1]) / 2.0f));
 32 |
 33 |	float edgeDistance[4];
 34 |	edgeDistance[0] = sum(edgePosition[0]);
 35 |
 36 |	/*
 37 |		Calcula aqu los niveles de teselacin
 38 |	*/
 39 |	if (gl_InvocationID == 0) {
 40 |		gl_TessLevelOuter[0] = 64.0 / max(edgeDistance[0], 1.0f);
 41 |		gl_TessLevelOuter[1] = 64.0 / max(edgeDistance[0], 1.0f);
 42 |		gl_TessLevelOuter[2] = 64.0 / max(edgeDistance[0], 1.0f);
 43 |		gl_TessLevelOuter[3] = 64.0 / max(edgeDistance[0], 1.0f);
 44 |
 45 |		gl_TessLevelInner[0] = 64.0 / max(edgeDistance[0], 1.0f);
 46 |		gl_TessLevelInner[1] = 64.0 / max(edgeDistance[0], 1.0f);
 47 |	}
 48 |}
 49 |

Tesselation control shader: ../p8/shader.tesc
---------------------------------------------
  1 |#version 420 core
  2 |
  3 |// Teselation control
  4 |
  5 |layout (vertices = 4) out;
  6 |
  7 |in VS_OUT {
  8 |	vec2 textureCoord;
  9 |} from_vs[];
 10 |
 11 |out TESC_OUT {
 12 |	vec2 textureCoord;
 13 |} to_tese[];
 14 |
 15 |
 16 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
 17 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
 18 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
 19 |  mat4 projMatrix;
 20 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
 21 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
 22 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 23 |};
 24 |
 25 |void main() {
 26 |	// Propagamos la posicin y la coordenada de textura al shader de evaluacin
 27 |	gl_out[gl_InvocationID].gl_Position = gl_in[gl_InvocationID].gl_Position;
 28 |	to_tese[gl_InvocationID].textureCoord = from_vs[gl_InvocationID].textureCoord;
 29 |
 30 |	// TODO Modificar altura en funcin a color imagen
 31 |	gl_out[gl_InvocationID].gl_Position.y = sum(texture(from_vs[gl_InvocationID].texUnitHeightMap, from_vs[gl_InvocationID].textureCoord).rrr)/3.0;
 32 |	
 33 |	vec3 edgePosition[4];
 34 |	float edgeDistance[4];
 35 |
 36 |	for (int i = 0; i < 4; i++) {
 37 |		edgePosition[i] = vec3(modelviewMatrix * ((gl_out[i].gl_Position + gl_out[(i+1)%4].gl_Position) / 2.0f));
 38 |		
 39 |		edgeDistance[i] = distance(edgePosition[i], vec3(0.0,0.0,0.0));
 40 |	}
 41 |
 42 |	/*
 43 |		Calcula aqu los niveles de teselacin
 44 |	*/
 45 |	if (gl_InvocationID == 0) {
 46 |		gl_TessLevelOuter[0] = 64.0 / max(edgeDistance[3], 1.0f);
 47 |		gl_TessLevelOuter[1] = 64.0 / max(edgeDistance[2], 1.0f);
 48 |		gl_TessLevelOuter[2] = 64.0 / max(edgeDistance[1], 1.0f);
 49 |		gl_TessLevelOuter[3] = 64.0 / max(edgeDistance[0], 1.0f);
 50 |
 51 |		gl_TessLevelInner[0] = (gl_TessLevelOuter[0] + gl_TessLevelOuter[2]) / 2.0f;
 52 |		gl_TessLevelInner[1] = (gl_TessLevelOuter[1] + gl_TessLevelOuter[3]) / 2.0f;
 53 |	}
 54 |}
 55 |
